***задвигать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:задвигать.html>задвига́ть</a> (20558)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:двигать.html>дви́гать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dvígatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:задвигать.html>задви́гать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zadvígatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:двигать.html>дви́гать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to start moving</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">задви́г-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zadvíg-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:задвигать.html>задвига́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zadvigátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:задвинуть.html>задви́нуть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to push (into), to slide (into) (e.g. curtains, drawer, etc.)</li></ol>

***задвижка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:задвижка.html>задви́жка</a> (16323)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">задви́г-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zadvíg-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:задвижка.html>задви́жка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zadvížka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:задвижка.html>задви́жки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:задвижка.html>задви́жки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:задвижка.html>задви́жек</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><i>(shutting)</i> bolt</li>
<li>door bolt</li>
<li>window catch</li>
<li>damper <i>(of a chimney)</i></li>
<li>slide valve
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:задвижка.html>задви́жка</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:трубопровод.html>трубопрово́да</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zadvížka</b> truboprovóda</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">pipeline valve</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:двинуть.html>дви́нуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dvínutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:задвинуть.html>задви́нуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zadvínutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:задвигать.html>задвига́ть</a></b>)

***задевать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:задевать.html>задева́ть</a> (7626)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:задевать.html>задева́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zadevátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:задеть.html>заде́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to touch, to brush <i>(against)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проехать.html>прое́хать</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:задеть.html>заде́в</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">projéxatʹ, ne zadév</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">to clear</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to be caught, to hit, to strike</li>
<li><i>(in a conversation, narration)</i> to touch <i>(upon)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to affect, to offend, to hurt
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:задевать.html>задева́ть</a></b> чьё-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:самолюбие.html>самолю́бие</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zadevátʹ</b> čʹjó-libo samoljúbije</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">to offend/wound smb's pride</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:задевать.html>задева́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:живой.html>живо́е</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">zadevátʹ za živóje</i> ― <span class="e-translation">cut to the quick; touch on the raw; touch a sore spot</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">medicine</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to affect
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жизненный.html>жи́зненно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:важный.html>ва́жные</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:орган.html>органы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бы́ли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:задетый.html>заде́ты</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">žíznenno vážnyje organy ne býli zadety</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">no vital organs were affected</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:задевать.html>задева́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zadevátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to mislay</li></ol>

***задействовать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:задействовать.html>заде́йствовать</a> (13100)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:действовать.html>де́йствовать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">déjstvovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:задействовать.html>заде́йствовать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zadéjstvovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>

***заделать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:заделать.html>заде́лать</a> (16542)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:делать.html>де́лать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">délatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заделать.html>заде́лать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zadélatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">заде́лывать</b>)
</p>

<li>to seal</li>
<li>to caulk</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:задержать.html>задержа́ть</a> (2170)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:держать.html>держа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">deržátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:задержать.html>задержа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zaderžátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:задерживать.html>заде́рживать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to detain, to hold back, to stop</li>
<li>to delay, to check</li>
<li>to arrest, to detain</li>
<li>to slow down, to retard, to delay, to hamper

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:задержаться.html>задержа́ться</a> (3778)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:задержать.html>задержа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zaderžátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:задержаться.html>задержа́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zaderžátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:задерживаться.html>заде́рживаться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to linger, to stay <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">too long</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:задержаться.html>задержи́тесь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:секунда.html>секу́нду</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Zaderžítesʹ</b> na sekúndu.</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>Stay</b> for a short time.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to be late, to be delayed</li>
<li>to linger (on, over)</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:задержать.html>задержа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zaderžátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:задерживать.html>заде́рживать</a> (6715)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:задержать.html>задержа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zaderžátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:задерживать.html>заде́рживать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zadérživatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:задержать.html>задержа́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to detain, to hold back, to stop</li>
<li>to delay, to check</li>
<li>to arrest, to detain</li>
<li>to slow down, to retard, to delay, to hamper
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:задерживать.html>заде́рживать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дыхание.html>дыха́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zadérživatʹ</b> dyxánije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to hold one's breath</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:задерживать.html>заде́рживать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zadérživatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:задерживаться.html>заде́рживаться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zadérživatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:задержаться.html>задержа́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to linger, to stay too long</li>
<li>to be late, to be delayed</li>
<li>to linger (on, over)</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:задерживать.html>заде́рживать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zadérživatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***задеть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:задеть.html>заде́ть</a> (5505)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:деть.html>деть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">detʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:задеть.html>заде́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zadétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:задевать.html>задева́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to touch, to brush <i>(against)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проехать.html>прое́хать</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:задеть.html>заде́в</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">projéxatʹ, ne <b>zadév</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">to clear</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to be caught, to hit, to strike</li>
<li><i>(in a conversation, narration)</i> to touch <i>(upon)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to affect, to offend, to hurt
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:задеть.html>заде́ть</a></b> чьё-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:самолюбие.html>самолю́бие</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zadétʹ</b> čʹjó-libo samoljúbije</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">to offend/wound smb's pride</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:задеть.html>заде́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:живой.html>живо́е</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">zadétʹ za živóje</i> ― <span class="e-translation">cut to the quick; touch on the raw; touch a sore spot</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">medicine</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to affect
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жизненный.html>жи́зненно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:важный.html>ва́жные</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:орган.html>органы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бы́ли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:задетый.html>заде́ты</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">žíznenno vážnyje organy ne býli zadety</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">no vital organs were affected</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***задирать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:задирать.html>задира́ть</a> (12317)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-дира́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-dirátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:задирать.html>задира́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zadirátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:задрать.html>задра́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to break, to split (skin, fingernails)</li>
<li>to lift, to pull up (head, nose, etc.)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to annoy badly</li></ol>

***задиристый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:задиристый.html>зади́ристый</a> (27032)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:задиристый.html>зади́ристый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zadíristyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)зади́ристее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)зади́ристей</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> cocky; quarrelsome; cheeky; blusterous</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зад.html>зад</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zad</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ний</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:задний.html>за́дний</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zádnij</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:более.html>бо́лее</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:задний.html>за́дний</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:самый.html>са́мый</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:задний.html>за́дний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>rear, back, hind
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:без.html>без</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:задний.html>за́дних</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:нога.html>ног</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">bez <b>zádnix</b> nog</i> ― <span class="e-translation">dead tired</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:без.html>без</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:задний.html>за́дних</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мысль.html>мы́слей</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">bez <b>zádnix</b> mýslej</i> ― <span class="e-translation">without ulterior motive</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гласный.html>гла́сные</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:задний.html>за́днего</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ряд.html>ря́да</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">glásnyje <b>zádnevo</b> rjáda</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>back</b> vowels (linguistics)</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
